\centerline{\footnotesize v\"aljaantud: J\"arvemetsal 2006.a.}

\noindent{\footnotesize Koostanud: \bf{Mart Kuhn, Arne Roomann-Kurrik, Liina Sarapik}}\\
{\footnotesize Palju t\"anu: \bf{Juhan Aavik, EELK, Tiina Ets, Tiina Fischgrund, M. Hunt, Leena Kangro, Erni Kilm, hr. \vspace{2in}
\noindent {\it ,,Laul olgu l\"uhike v\~oi pikk, peaasi et on \~opetlik.``}
\cleardoublepage
{\samepage\raggedbottom
\raggedright
\sloppy
\centerline{ {\bf {\large Legend lakewoodi valgest liivast.}}}
\vspace{0.1in}
\hrule height 0.05ex
\vspace{0.1in}
\centerline{ {\em {\footnotesize nskm. Jyri Kork'i kirjutatud kogudest}}}}
\vspace{.05in}

Lakewoodi valge liiv on tagasihoidlik nagu s\~onajala \~ois.  Teda ei leidu laia juttu ajavas rahvahulgas Piprapoe leti ees.  Teda pole v\~oimalik n\"aha keskp\"aeva l\~o\~omavas p\"aikeses gaidide supluspaigas j\"arve kaldal.  Ja teda ei n\"ae iial need linnalapsed, kes kolmehobuj\~oulise taskulambiga \"o\"osel pimestavad k\~oiki vastutulejaid.  Lakewoodi valge liiv helendab \"uksikuil metsaradadel.  Ta muutub seda valgemaks, mida s\"ugavamaks s\"uveneb \"o\"o.  S\~obralikult juhib ta iga skaudipoissi ja gaidit\"udrukut, kes ainult kuu v\~oi t\"ahtede valgusel s\"aeb oma hiliseid samme.  Kuid k\~oige valgem on ta siiski talvistes laagrim\"alestustes.  Ja see Lakewoodi valge liiv on pealegi n\~oiutud liiv!  Sellest liivast v\~oib leida kulda.  Neid kullateri on loomulikult palju-palju raskem otsida, kui valget liiva ennast.  Aga ometi leitakse neid ja viiakse koju kaasa.

Mismoodi n\"aevad v\"alja need kullaterad?

\"Uks naerun\"aoline m\"alestus, millest emale ei r\"a\"agita, aga mis soojendab s\"udant kogu koolitalve.  \"Uks uus s\~oprus, s\~olmitud kahe teineteisest tuhandete miilide kaugusel elava eesti skaudipoisi vahel kes varjasid end samas kadakap\~o\~osas laagripolitsei ja gaidlaagri juhi eest.  \"Uks hiilga vahva laul, mida \~opiti vihmas suitseva ja susiseva l\~okke juures, kui juht l\"aks magama.

Jah, Lakewoodis on olemas valge liiv!

\hfill
Jyri Kork, nskm.

  \index{The Star-Spangled Banner}
  \vspace{0.2in}
    \centerline{
      \bfseries
      \large The Star-Spangled Banner
    }
  \nopagebreak[4]
  \vspace{0.1in}
  \nopagebreak[4]
  \hrule height 0.05ex
  \nopagebreak[4]
  \vspace{-0.05in}

  {\footnotesize F. S. Key \hfill J. S. Smith }\\
  \vspace{0.01in}



  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.01in }{ 0.0in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] O say, can you see, by the dawn's early light, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] What so proudly we hailed at the twilight's last gleaming? \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Whose broad stripes and bright stars, through the perilous fight, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] O'er the ramparts we watched, were so gallantly streaming! \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] And the rockets' red glare, the bombs bursting in air, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Gave proof through the night that our flag was still there: \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] O say, does that star-spangled banner yet wave \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] O'er the land of the free and the home of the brave? \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.01in }{ 0.0in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] On the shore, dimly seen through the mists of the deep, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Where the foe's haughty host in dread silence reposes, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] What is that which the breeze, o'er the towering steep, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] As it fitfully blows, now conceals, now discloses? \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Now it catches the gleam of the morning's first beam, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] In full glory reflected now shines on the stream: \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] 'Tis the star-spangled banner! O long may it wave \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] O'er the land of the free and the home of the brave! \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.01in }{ 0.0in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] And where is that band who so vauntingly swore \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] That the havoc of war and the battle's confusion \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] A home and a country should leave us no more? \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Their blood has washed out their foul footsteps' pollution. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] No refuge could save the hireling and slave \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] From the terror of flight, or the gloom of the grave: \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] And the star-spangled banner in triumph doth wave \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] O'er the land of the free and the home of the brave! \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.01in }{ 0.0in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Oh! thus be it ever, when freemen shall stand \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Between their loved homes and the war's desolation! \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Blest with victory and peace, may the Heaven-rescued land \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Praise the Power that hath made and preserved us a nation. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Then conquer we must, when our cause it is just, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] And this be our motto: ``In God is our trust.'' \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] And the star-spangled banner in triumph shall wave \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] O'er the land of the free and the home of the brave! \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
}

  \index{Nii ajaratas ringi k\"aind}

  \index{Ajaratas}
  \vspace{0.2in}

      \bfseries
      \large Ajaratas
    }
  \nopagebreak[4]

  \vspace{0.01in}



  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.8in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Nii ajaratas ringi k\"ain'd, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] me kaunid p\"aevad m\"o\"oda l\"ain'd, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] :,: meil tuleb lahkuda. :,: \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Meid lahkumine kurvaks teeb \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] ja s\"uda p\~oues nukralt l\"o\"ob \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] :,: ja hinges raske mul. :,: \\
  }

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] On palju murtud piikisid \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] k\"ull vastu tema m\"u\"urisid. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Kui l\~oppes aga s\~ojatants \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] j\"ai v\~oitjaks Kalevite kants! \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.9in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Ta tornid paistvad kaugele, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] nii maale kui ka merele. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Kui oled k\"ainud v\~o\~oraid teid, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] l\"o\"ob s\"uda kiirelt, kui n\"aed neid. \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.9in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] On ilmas palju neidusid, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] neist kaunid on nii m\~onedki. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Kuid kaunimad on elamas \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] me armsas vanas Tallinnas. \\
  }

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Sinu k\"asi, Jeesus Krist. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Kas ma v\"asin \~ohtul hilja, \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] surres maitsen eluvilja \\

  {\em {\footnotesize (Viisil: ,,Lucky Lips{``}) } }

  \pagebreak[1]

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] tean mis v\"a\"art on mehe m\"uts. \\

  \end{changemargin}

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] peaasi kikilips! \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Kikilips teeb mehe \v{s}ikiks, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] kikilipsu p\"uhaks pean. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Kikilipsuga siin ilmas \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] k\~oik ma k\"atte saan. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Kikilips teeb lahti uksed, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] murrab lahti s\"udamed. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Ei kikilipsu vastu saa \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] siin maa peal keegi veel. \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] pruun v\~oi punane v\~oi must. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Ta ei heida sulle varju, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] pigem kaunistab sind just. \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] ja sa k\"usid minult miks, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] siis vastan \"upris veendunult: \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] tuli mul kord piibuhimu, umpa, umpa jaa. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] :,: Piibu tegin kasek\"asnast, umpa, umpa jaa. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Tubakakoti lambanahast, umpa, umpa jaa. :,: \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] vanataadi tubakalehti, umpa, umpa jaa, \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] v\"aike \~ode j\"arel jooksis, umpa, umpa jaa. \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] tikust tule peale l\"aitsin, umpa, umpa jaa. \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] ja neid piibu sisse toppis, umpa, umpa jaa. \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] sammud linnast v\"alja seame! \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] gaididel on vaba aeg. \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] metsa sammume, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] laagripaika j\~ouame. \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Kui on \~oiglane gaide oma m\~otetes, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] siis takistust pole tal ees. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] V\"aike seiklus ei h\"airi me rahu, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] ainus tingimus on vaid see: \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] kui on l\~opnud seik, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] kurgus nutumaik, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] \"ara sellest v\"aljagi tee! \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}

  \index{Olen gaid ja kodumaa t\"utar}

      \large Olen gaid ja kodumaa t\"utar
    }
  \nopagebreak[4]

  \nopagebreak[4]

  \nopagebreak[4]
  \vspace{-0.05in}




  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.7in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Olen gaid ja kodumaa t\"utar, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] alati j\"a\"an truuks isamaal. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Tihti r\"annates v\~o\~oramaa pinnal, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] m\~otted lendavad kodumaa raal. \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 1.0in }{ 0.1in }
  {

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] %REFRAIN \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Seistes \"uksinda kaljusel rannal, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] kus mu vannet on kuulamas laas, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] v\"aike kodu, sind s\"udames kannan, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] kuni saatuselt tagasi su saan. \\
  }

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Silmades s\"adelev \~onn \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] p\"aikesest s\"aravam on. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Teotahtest k\"ates on ramm, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] \~oigluse radadel on samm. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Rivis me sammume sirges ja pikas - \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] elu on gaidile r\~o\~omuderikas. \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] meie p\"aralt lai maailm. \\

    }

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Leegi kuma puieladvus k\~orgele. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Kutsu kokku gaide l\~okketulele. \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 1.0in }{ 0.1in }

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] %REFRAIN \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] S\"uti, s\"uti, s\"uti, s\"uti. \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] m\"alestuste rajale. \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] varba veriseks l\~oin. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Kaks k\"a\"aru v\~oileiba s\~oin, \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] paadist kaotasin m\~ola. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Kaugelt kostis karjakella k\~ola, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] meeles ikka see p\"aev! \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Laula mulle seda vana viit, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] mis kord ema laulis meil. \\
  }

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] nii kuulas v\"aikene mees \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] pea paistmas patjade seest. \\

      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] ja poisi v\"asinud p\"ai \\

  \index{Vangile ei meeldi trellid}
  \vspace{0.2in}
    \centerline{
      \bfseries
      \large Vangile ei meeldi trellid
    }
  \nopagebreak[4]
  \vspace{0.1in}
  \nopagebreak[4]
  \hrule height 0.05ex
  \nopagebreak[4]
  \vspace{-0.05in}




  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.8in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Vangile ei meeldi trellid, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] s\~oduril ei meeldi miin, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] arstile ei meeldi haiged, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] ja haigele ei meeldi piin. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] President ei kuula rahvast, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] rahvale ei meeldi vaht, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] vanale ei meeldi noored, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] ja minule ei meeldi praht. \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 1.1in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] %REFRAIN \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Mulle meeldib naer, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] mulle meeldib armastus, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] mulle meeldib k\~oik see, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] mis meie sees on kaunist veel. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Mulle meeldib puutumatu loodus, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] meeldib olla noor, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] ja oma rahvaga mul meeldib olla koos! \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.8in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] \clearpage M\~onele ei meeldi ausus, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] m\~onele ei meeldi kuld, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] m\~onele ei meeldi minevik, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] ja m\~onele kodune muld. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Tulijatel k\~oik on v\~o\~oras, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] olijatel kaob kultuur, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] minejatel muutub m\"alu, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] ja v\"aikest \~ogib ahnelt suur. \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 1.1in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] %REFRAIN \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Mulle meeldib naer \ldots \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.8in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Pankurid ei seedi vaeseid, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] vaestele ei meeldi v\~oim, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] preestrile ei meeldi saatan, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] ja saatanale v\~o\~oras h\~oim. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Targale ei meeldi lollide jutt, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] koerale ei meeldi rihm, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] n\~omedus ei seedi m\~oistuse h\"a\"alt, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] ja mulle ei meeldi tugenev vihm. \\

    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] \"O\"o pime ja paat l\~oikab vahutavat merd, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] silmapiirilt kaob Eestimaa rand. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] :,: J\"alle Maarjamaa pinnal voolab sangarite verd, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] mida r\~ohunud lubjavildi kand. :,: \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.1in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Armas Eesti, anna andeks et sust lahkuma ma pean, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] kuid m\"alestus sinust mulle j\"a\"ab. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] :,: \~Oitseb sirel, saabun tagasi, seda kindlasti n\"u\"ud tean, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] annan sulle oma relvastatud k\"ae. :,: \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.1in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Armas Taaraisa, juhi Soome sepa poole teed, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] sealt saame me relvi ja n\~ou. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] :,: Meie esiisad aastasadu k\"ainud seda teed, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] neid ei kohutanud tormised veed. :,: \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.1in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Ei Eesti pinnal iial kasva v\~o\~ora riigi taim, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] ei pooleli j\"a\"a Lembitu t\"o\"o. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] :,: Ei punalipud sini-musta-valget katta saa, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] ei iial ei kordu Juri\"o\"o. :,: \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
}
\vskip 0in plus 1in minus 0in
\vspace{-0.05in}
\pagebreak[3]
\vspace{ 0.1in }
{
  \samepage
  \raggedbottom
  \raggedright
  \sloppy


  \index{\"Uhte laulu}
  \vspace{0.2in}
    \centerline{
      \bfseries
      \large \"Uhte laulu
    }
  \nopagebreak[4]
  \vspace{0.1in}
  \nopagebreak[4]
  \hrule height 0.05ex
  \nopagebreak[4]
  \vspace{-0.05in}




  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.4in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] \"Uhte laulu tahaks laulda, \"uhte ainukest. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Mis kui v\"agev merelaine kerkiks s\"udamest. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Mis kui v\"agev merelaine veereks \"ule maa. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Tungiks l\"abi rahva hingest, keelata ei sa. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Tungiks l\"abi rahva hingest, t\~ouseks meeste meel. \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.4in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] V\"alguksid siis vaimum\~o\~ogad suurte t\"o\"ode teel. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] V\"alguksid siis vaimum\~o\~ogad kodutaeva all. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Kumaksid \"o\"od kuldsemini t\"ahed \"uleval. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] \"Uhte laulu tahaks laulda, \"uhte ainukest. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Mis kui v\"agev merelaine kerkiks s\"udamest. \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.4in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] La-la-la-la-la-la\ldots \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
}

  \index{\"Uks mees n\"agi unes taevalikku \~oiglust}

      \bfseries
      \large \"Uks mees n\"agi unes taevalikku \~oiglust
    }
  \nopagebreak[4]
  \vspace{0.1in}
  \nopagebreak[4]
  \hrule height 0.05ex

  \vspace{-0.05in}

    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.1in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] \"Uks mees n\"agi unes taevalikku \~oiglust, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] mis \"uhendab k\~oik, kes tema eest v\~oitlevad. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] \"Uks mees n\"agi unes taevalikku \~oiglust, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] ja sellest p\"aevast peale hakkas seda kuulutama. \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.4in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] %REFRAIN \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] Kuid ah --- \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] L\~opuks on k\~oik ainult enesem\"u\"umine, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] turul me oleme vennad ja \~oed. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] P\"aevhaaval, tundhaaval, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] t\"ukkhaaval, jupphaaval \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] \"uksteisele m\"u\"ume \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] omad usud ja t\~oed\ldots \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
  \pagebreak[1]
    \begin{changemargin}{ 0.1in }{ 0.1in }
  {
    \small
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] \"Uks naine n\"agi unes taevalikku armastust, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] mis lunastab k\~oik, kes temasse usuvad. \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] \"Uks naine n\"agi unes taevalikku armastust, \\
      \noindent \nopagebreak[4] ja sellest p\"aevast peale hakkas seda kuuluama. \\
  }
  \end{changemargin}
